   "source": [
    "from theano import shared\n",
    "import keras\n",
    "from keras.models import Sequential\n",
    "from keras.layers import Dense, BatchNormalization\n",
    "\n",
    "def get_params(model):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Get parameters and updates from Keras model\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    shared_in_updates = list()\n",
    "    params = list()\n",
    "    updates = dict()\n",
    "    \n",
    "    for l in model.layers:\n",
    "        attrs = dir(l)\n",
    "        # Updates\n",
    "        if 'updates' in attrs:\n",
    "            updates.update(l.updates)\n",
    "            shared_in_updates += [e[0] for e in l.updates]\n",
    "        \n",
    "        # Shared variables\n",
    "        for attr_str in attrs:\n",
    "            attr = getattr(l, attr_str)\n",
    "            if type(attr) is tt.sharedvar.TensorSharedVariable:\n",
    "                if attr is not model.get_input_at(0):\n",
    "                    params.append(attr)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    return list(set(params) - set(shared_in_updates)), updates\n",
    "\n",
    "# This code is required when using BatchNormalization layer\n",
    "keras.backend.theano_backend._LEARNING_PHASE = \\\n",
    "    shared(np.uint8(1), name='keras_learning_phase')"
   ]
  },

    "from keras.layers import Input, Dense\n",
    "\n",
    "class GaussWeights(object):\n",
    "    def __init__(self):\n",
    "        self.count = 0\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __call__(self, shape, name='w'):\n",
    "        #import pdb; pdb.set_trace()\n",
    "        return pm.Normal(\n",
    "            name, mu=0, sd=.1,\n",
    "            testval=np.random.normal(size=shape).astype(np.float64),\n",
    "            shape=shape)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def build_ann(x, y, init):\n",
    "    with pm.Model() as model:\n",
    "        keras_model = Sequential()\n",
    "        keras_model.add(Input(tensor=x, shape=(x.get_value().shape[1],)))\n",
    "        keras_model.add(Dense(5, init=init, activation='tanh'))\n",
    "        keras_model.add(Dense(5, init=init, activation='tanh'))\n",
    "        keras_model.add(Dense(1, init=init, activation='sigmoid'))\n",
    "        \n",
    "        b = pm.Bernoulli(\"p\", p=keras_model[:, 0], observed=y)\n",
    "    return model\n",
    "\n",
    "ann_input = theano.shared(X.astype(np.float64))\n",
    "ann_output = theano.shared(Y.astype(np.float64))\n",
    "\n",
    "neural_network = build_ann(ann_input, ann_output, GaussWeights())"
   ]

    "### Uncertainty in predicted value\n",
    "\n",
    "So far, everything I showed we could have done with a non-Bayesian Neural Network. The mean of the posterior predictive for each class-label should be identical to maximum likelihood predicted values. However, we can also look at the standard deviation of the posterior predictive to get a sense for the uncertainty in our predictions. Here is what that looks like:"

    "cmap = sns.cubehelix_palette(light=1, as_cmap=True)\n",
    "fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n",
    "contour = ax.contourf(*grid, ppc['p'].std(axis=0).reshape(100, 100), cmap=cmap)\n",

   "source": [
    "We can see that very close to the decision boundary, our uncertainty as to which label to predict is highest. You can imagine that associating predictions with uncertainty is a critical property for many applications like health care. To further maximize accuracy, we might want to train the model primarily on samples from that high-uncertainty region."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## Mini-batch ADVI: Scaling data size\n",
    "\n",
    "So far, we have trained our model on all data at once. Obviously this won't scale to something like ImageNet. Moreover, training on mini-batches of data (stochastic gradient descent) avoids local minima and can lead to faster convergence.\n",
    "\n",
    "Fortunately, ADVI can be run on mini-batches as well. It just requires some setting up:"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": false
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# Set back to original data to retrain\n",
    "ann_input.set_value(X_train)\n",
    "ann_output.set_value(Y_train)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Tensors and RV that will be using mini-batches\n",
    "minibatch_tensors = [ann_input, ann_output]\n",
    "minibatch_RVs = [out]\n",
    "\n",
    "# Generator that returns mini-batches in each iteration\n",
    "def create_minibatch(data):\n",
    "    rng = np.random.RandomState(0)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    while True:\n",
    "        # Return random data samples of set size 100 each iteration\n",
    "        ixs = rng.randint(len(data), size=50)\n",
    "        yield data[ixs]\n",
    "\n",
    "minibatches = zip(\n",
    "    create_minibatch(X_train), \n",
    "    create_minibatch(Y_train),\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "total_size = len(Y_train)"
   ]
  }
